                  <h2 data-v-2c6ed106="">Text Editor</h2>
                </div>

                  <div
                    data-v-5da8bb0e=""
                    autocomplete="off"
                    autocorrect="off"
                    autocapitalize="none"
                    spellcheck="false"
                    contenteditable="true"
                    class="inner-content texteditorform"
                  >
                    CliniQ.OS FM was conceived one awfully rainy summer in the Highlands of Scotland - a virtual vacation, if you will. The audio and
                    video streams are curated to inject a healthy dose of serotonin into your brain.
                    <br data-v-5da8bb0e="" />
                    <br data-v-5da8bb0e="" />
                    Our Instagram account,
                    <span data-v-5da8bb0e="" contenteditable="false">
                      <a data-v-5da8bb0e="" href="https://www.instagram.com/CliniQ.OS" target="blank">@CliniQ.OS</a>
                    </span>
                    , is curated with a similar mindset.
                    <br data-v-5da8bb0e="" />
                    <br data-v-5da8bb0e="" />
                    Thanks for visiting, we hope you'll grab a sun lounger and stick around.
                    <br data-v-5da8bb0e="" />
